(Top to bottom) • People who read the Manga first • People who used to read literature and accidentally stumbled upon BSD (manga or Anime) • People who watched the Anime because of accidentally discovering it and now read the Manga • People who watched JUST the anime , but for the plot • Any ship related viewers
